The client is self-contained and does not open any network ports on the device.\r\n\r\n* DOES IT OPEN A LOCAL PORT ON THE PI?\r\nNo. Client connections are initiated from the device end and do not open any local ports.\r\n\r\n* DO I NEED TO INSTALL SOMETHING ON THE PI?\r\nYes, you need to install the Dataplicity agent on the Pi. You can view the source on GitHub.\r\n\r\n* DOES DATAPLICITY AGENT RUN AS ROOT?\r\nNo. When you log into the Dataplicity shell you still need to explicitly ask for super user rights to gain full control.","ProductFamilyName":"Apps","Schema":"Card;1"}],"Title":"أهم العناصر المجانية","HasThirdPartyIAPs":false,"AlgoName":"RECO-Algo-Version","AlgoValue":"Lists;topFree;;Apps;00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000003","TotalItems":991,"PageSize":200}}
